Usage: nmcli connection modify { ARGUMENTS | help }

ARGUMENTS := [id | uuid | path] <ID> ([+|-]<setting>.<property> <value>)+

Modify one or more properties of the connection profile.
The profile is identified by its name, UUID or D-Bus path. For multi-valued
properties you can use optional '+' or '-' prefix to the property name.
The '+' sign allows appending items instead of overwriting the whole value.
The '-' sign allows removing selected items instead of the whole value.

ARGUMENTS := remove <setting>

Remove a setting from the connection profile.

Examples:
nmcli con mod home-wifi wifi.ssid rakosnicek
nmcli con mod em1-1 ipv4.method manual ipv4.addr "192.168.1.2/24, 10.10.1.5/8"
nmcli con mod em1-1 +ipv4.dns 8.8.4.4
nmcli con mod em1-1 -ipv4.dns 1
nmcli con mod em1-1 -ipv6.addr "abbe::cafe/56"
nmcli con mod bond0 +bond.options mii=500
nmcli con mod bond0 -bond.options downdelay
nmcli con mod em1-1 remove sriov

NM-SETTINGS-NMCLI(5)             Configuration            NM-SETTINGS-NMCLI(5)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       nm-settings-nmcli - Description of settings and properties of[m
       NetworkManager connection profiles for nmcli[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       NetworkManager is based on a concept of connection profiles, sometimes[m
       referred to as connections only. These connection profiles contain a[m
       network configuration. When NetworkManager activates a connection[m
       profile on a network device the configuration will be applied and an[m
       active network connection will be established. Users are free to create[m
       as many connection profiles as they see fit. Thus they are flexible in[m
       having various network configurations for different networking needs.[m
[m
       NetworkManager provides an API for configuring connection profiles, for[m
       activating them to configure the network, and inspecting the current[m
       network configuration. The command line tool [4mnmcli[24m is a client[m
       application to NetworkManager that uses this API. See [1mnmcli[22m(1) for[m
       details.[m
[m
       With commands like nmcli connection add, nmcli connection modify and[m
       nmcli connection show, connection profiles can be created, modified and[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       inspected. A profile consists of properties. On D-Bus this follows the[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       format as described by [1mnm-settings-dbus[22m(5), while this manual page[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       describes the settings format how they are expected by [4mnmcli[24m.[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 5 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       The settings and properties shown in tables below list all available[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       connection configuration options. However, note that not all settings[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       are applicable to all connection types.  [4mnmcli[24m connection editor has[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       also a built-in [4mdescribe[24m command that can display description of[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       particular settings and properties of this page.[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 10 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 11 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       The [4msetting[24m and [4mproperty[24m can be abbreviated provided they are unique.[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 12 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       The list below also shows aliases that can be used unqualified instead[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 13 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       of the full name. For example connection.interface-name and ifname[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 14 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       refer to the same property.[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 15 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 16 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K   [1mconnection setting[0m[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 17 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       General Connection Profile Settings.[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 18 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 19 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       Properties:[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 20 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 21 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K       [1mauth-retries[0m[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 22 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K           The number of retries for the authentication. Zero means to try[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 23 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K           indefinitely; -1 means to use a global default. If the global[m
[7m Manual page nm-settings(5) line 24 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[KBB[K           default is not set, the authentication retries for 3 times before[m
